# Roadmap

Work top-to-bottom; `/dev-cycle` picks the first unchecked item. Check items off as they land (with tests). Keep milestones honest ŌĆö an item isn't done until it works in the running app **and** over the control protocol.

## M0 ŌĆö Foundation Ō£ģ
- [x] Repo scaffold, docs, agent fleet, skills
- [x] SPM monorepo: DAWCore / DAWEngine / DAWControl / AIServices / DAWApp
- [x] Domain model v0 (project, tracks, clips, transport, mixer state)
- [x] Control WebSocket server skeleton + command router
- [x] MCP server skeleton with core tool surface
- [x] App shell: dark theme, transport bar, glowing meter component

## M1 ŌĆö Core audio engine Ō£ģ
- [x] Audio file import (wav/aiff/mp3/m4a) onto tracks
- [x] Sample-accurate multitrack playback via engine graph
- [x] Transport: play/stop/seek/loop region, position broadcast to UI + control clients
- [x] Per-track and master metering (peak/RMS) driving the glow meters
- [x] Master volume, per-track volume/pan/mute/solo wired to engine
- [x] Offline render (mixdown to wav) ŌĆö `render.mixdown` command
- [x] Engine test harness: offline-render assertions (null test, gain test) ŌĆö determinism null (exact 0.0) + unity-vs-source + gain suite; golden-master null noted as future addition

## M2 ŌĆö Recording & project persistence
- [x] Record from default input onto armed tracks (`track.setArm`, `transport.record`, host-time-aligned takes) ŌĆö no round-trip latency compensation yet (M4 PDC)
- [x] Input device enumeration/selection (`input.listDevices`, `input.setDevice`) ŌĆö pinned-device capture fixed 2026-07-05 (benign config-change triage + first-buffer watchdog; live E2E green for default-uid pin, ZoomAudioDevice pin, and unpinned)
- [x] Punch in/out windows (`transport.setPunch`, writer accept-window)
- [x] Metronome/click with count-in
- [x] `.dawproj` bundle format: versioned JSON + media dir; open/save/autosave
- [x] Undo/redo across all commands (coalescing snapshot journal in DAWCore; `edit.undo`/`edit.redo`, Edit-menu ŌīśZ/Ōć¦ŌīśZ)

## M3 ŌĆö MIDI & instruments
- [x] (i) MIDI domain + commands ŌĆö `Clip.notes` payload (`MIDINote`: pitch/velocity/startBeat/lengthBeats, clamped, canonically ordered, mutually exclusive with audio media); `clip.addMIDI` / `clip.setNotes` / `clip.remove` on the control protocol (whole-array note set, per-clip undo coalescing); additive v1 persistence; instrument-track-only rule
- [x] (ii) Piano-roll editor (Simple + Pro views) ŌĆö note draw/move/resize/velocity, snap grid, driving `clip.setNotes`; timeline clip lanes + `debug.captureUI` self-render verification
- [x] (iii) Sample-accurate MIDI scheduler ŌĆö settles the sequencer clock decision (one `AVAudioSourceNode` per instrument track; host-delta live epoch / latched offline epoch), lock-free event delivery via an immutable schedule behind a C11 atomic pointer (`CAtomics` shim, Ōēź1 s retire bin), all-notes-off flush flag on every stop/seek/tempo/loop-wrap/reschedule, `InstrumentRendering` seam (AU-shaped for M3 vi) with EventCaptureInstrument + TestToneInstrument; validated by frame-exact offline event-timestamp tests
- [x] (iv) Built-in poly synth ŌĆö 16-voice subtractive synth (PolyBLEP saw/square, triangle, sine; linear ADSR; Simper SVF low-pass) behind `InstrumentRendering`; `Track.instrument: InstrumentDescriptor?` (additive, nil ŌćÆ polySynth default), `track.setInstrument` control command + `track_set_instrument` MCP tool with partial-update semantics; RT-safe in-place param changes (atomic POD publish, held notes survive), kind switch = node rebuild + reschedule
- [x] (v) Built-in sampler ŌĆö key zones (`SamplerZone`: audio file, root pitch, span, gain) under the same `InstrumentDescriptor`; pitched playback via linear-interp resampling (2^(╬ösemitones/12) ├Ś rate ratio), one-shot mode, anti-click attack/release; zones structural (rebuild) vs scalars in-place (atomic); zone media joins the `.dawproj` bundle copy (relative `media/` refs, dedupe, `mediaFilesCopied`); `sampler` object on `track.setInstrument` + MCP
- [x] (vi-a) AU instrument hosting (headless) ŌĆö `HostedAUInstrument` adapter behind the `InstrumentRendering` seam (our scheduler stays the only clock; events via `scheduleMIDIEventBlock` at in-quantum offsets; flush ŌåÆ CC123+120), `AUHostRegistry` (timeout-raced async prepare, strict-select/graceful-load: missing AU ŌåÆ silent placeholder + `status`), descriptor kind `audioUnit` with component identity + fullState base64 in `.dawproj`, `instrument.listAudioUnits` + `track.setInstrument audioUnit:` + MCP; `renderMixdown` now async (offline renders instantiate fresh AU instances); out-of-process AUv3 reliability deferred to M9 app bundling
- [x] (vi-b) AU plugin UI windows ŌĆö `requestViewController`/v2 view hosting in floating glass-chrome windows; open/close over the control protocol ŌĆö split 2026-07-10 per `docs/research/design-vi-b-au-windows.md` (DESIGN SETTLED ŌĆö the implementation contract; unblocked by pkg-a's real app bundle):
  - [x] (vi-b-1) Plumbing + generic body ŌĆö engine accessors for the live `AUAudioUnit` (concrete-class-only boundary exception) + registry `onRelease` invalidation seam; `plugin.openUI/closeUI/listOpenUIs` through a typed async `PluginUIControlling` seam (headless-honest errors); `PluginWindowLedger` (DAWAppKit, headless) + `PluginWindowManager`/`NSPanel` glass chrome (cyan/neutral, never violet); `AUGenericViewController` body only; `debug.captureUI {target:"plugin"}`; mixer/instrument open-window buttons; 3 MCP tools; headless suites + orchestrator live gate on system AUs (DLSMusicDevice/AUDelay), fully provable on the bare binary
  - [x] (vi-b-2) Vendor views ŌĆö full resolution ladder (`requestViewController` w/ 5 s once-gate timeout race ŌåÆ v2 `kAudioUnitProperty_CocoaUI` via `AUAudioUnitV2Bridge` + `AUViewProbe` in DAWEngine ŌåÆ `AUGenericViewController` fallback, never-failing), `BodyHostViewController` wrapping the vendor `AUCocoaUIBase` view, v3 `preferredContentSize` sizing + `frameDidChangeNotification` resize-follow (reentrancy-guarded, clamped in-bounds); ┬¦10 de-risk spike resolved by inventory (NO AUv3 installed ŌĆö the out-of-process AUv3 custom-view leg is SKIPPED-recorded, never faked); live gate on system units proves both branches ŌĆö DLSMusicDevice/AUDelay ŌåÆ `body:"custom"` (real vendor views inside our chrome), AUMatrixReverb ŌåÆ `body:"generic"` ŌĆö bare binary AND `dist/DAWPro.app` bundle identity; `docs/PACKAGING.md` note
- [x] (vii) MIDI hardware input ŌĆö CoreMIDI UMP protocol-1.0 port, omni-connect + hot-plug; live thru on armed instrument tracks via per-renderer SPSC rings behind an atomic fanout (offset-0 events, works while stopped, drop-newest + flush-on-drop so notes can't stick); recording shares the audio take's `PlaybackAnchor` beat math and lands MIDI clips in the same "Record Take N" undo step (punch trims audio only, v0); `midi.listInputs` + snapshot `midiInputs`/`midiEventCount` + MCP; hardware-free verification via virtual sources (`scripts/e2e-midi-record.swift`)

## M4 ŌĆö Mixer & FX suite
- [x] (i) Bus routing & sends ŌĆö bus tracks become real mix destinations: track output routing (master or bus), per-track sends (pre/post fader, level) into buses, bus volume/pan/mute/solo/meters in the engine graph + offline render parity; `track.setOutput` / `track.addSend|setSend|removeSend` commands + MCP + tests ŌĆö **COMPLETE 2026-07-06**: the parked mid-play send-activation defect resolved (stale render-clock anchor after the rewire bounce, one-flag fix ŌĆö see the RESOLVED entry under ## Blocked); live bus E2E 19/19 (a send added mid-play meters on its bus with NO transport command: within ~0.3 s for audio material, at the next note-on/loop wrap for MIDI material per the settled no-chase contract)
- [x] (ii) FX insert-chain architecture ŌĆö `EffectRendering` seam + `ChainHostAU` (in-process registered AU `aufx/dwch/DAWP`, spike-proven from the SPM binary) as a permanent per-strip insert point; chain edits are atomically published snapshots, NEVER graph mutations (the M4 (i) failure class eliminated by construction ŌĆö verified live: mid-play add/bypass/reorder/param with zero transport interruption); pre-fader inserts on audio/instrument/bus strips; `fx.add|remove|reorder|setBypass|setParam|describe` + 6 MCP tools; GainEffect proves the seam (bit-exact chain math); PDC-ready latency reporting (0 in v0)
- [x] (iii) Built-in FX pack 1 (dynamics & tone) ŌĆö 4-band parametric EQ (RBJ biquads, TDF2 Float64, 0 dB bands bit-exact-skipped), soft-knee stereo-linked compressor (real peak detector, log-domain gain computer), 5 ms-lookahead brickwall limiter (monotonic-deque window max; `|out| Ōēż ceiling` for EVERY sample by construction; first nonzero `latencySamples`, plumbed engineŌåÆstoreŌåÆwire per-effect); spectrum display deferred to mixer UI (vi)
- [x] (iv) Built-in FX pack 2 (space & color) ŌĆö Freeverb reverb (8 damped combs + 4 allpasses/channel, pre-delay, mid/side width), stereo delay (integer lines, echo at exactly round(timeMs├Śrate/1000), feedback high-cut, ping-pong crossfeed), tanh saturator (ŌłÆdriveDb/2 dB fixed compensation, odd harmonics at H2/H3Ōēł1e-15), stereo-linked gate (bit-exact passthrough open, true zeros closed, attack/hold/release ramps), 2-voice chorus (90┬░ stereo / 180┬░ inter-voice sine LFO offsets); all atomic-POD-publish RT-safe; 9 kinds on `fx.describe` + MCP; verified live (delay echoes in bounce, mid-play reverb add, ŌłÆ1 dB gate silence, 5-kind persistence)
- [x] (v) AU effect hosting (headless) ŌĆö `HostedAUEffect` pull-render adapter behind `EffectRendering` (in-place via stash box + preallocated scratch ABL, render failure ŌåÆ dry passthrough); registry reuses the instrument timeout-raced prepare with strict-select on add / placeholder+warning on load; async prepare ŌåÆ single-strip invalidate ŌåÆ chain republish (never a graph rebuild); real `latencySamples` from `au.latency` (AUPeakLimiter: 96 @ 48 kHz); fullState in `.dawproj`; `fx.add kind=audioUnit` + `fx.listAudioUnits` + MCP (47 tools); found+fixed AUv2-bridge input-bus-disabled bug; plugin UI windows stay gated on M9 bundling
- [x] (vi) Full mixer view ŌĆö console-style horizontal rack: channel strips (kind badge, inserts w/ bypass dots, sends w/ mini-faders, output picker, pan knob, long-throw fader w/ dB readout, mute/solo/arm glow buttons, live meter), BUSES-divided bus strips, accent-bordered pinned MASTER w/ stereo meter; `MixerModel` headless view-model in DAWAppKit (strip derivation/dB/pan/geometry, 10 tests); ARRANGEŌćäMIX header toggle + `ui.showMixer` debug-tier command; Canvas controls (VerticalFader/PanKnob/SendMiniFader); design language codified as the "Mixer console" pattern in DESIGN-LANGUAGE.md; verified by captureUI self-render (agent + independent) ŌĆö master insert chain deferred until DAWCore grows a master effect chain; hosted-AU insert picker UI deferred (control-plane add works)
- [x] (vii-a) Automation domain model + store CRUD ŌĆö `AutomationLane/Target/Point/Curve` in DAWCore (target enum persistence-stable incl. deferred sendLevel; pure `value(atBeat:)` evaluator, canonicalized points, clamp-through-target-range), `Track.automation` additive Codable, ProjectStore CRUD (idempotent addLane w/ v0 rejections, whole-array setPoints w/ 4096 cap + `automation.points:<laneID>` coalescing, cascades drop targeting lanes inside removeEffect/removeSend/bus-delete edits), `.dawproj` persistence omitted-when-empty (pre-automation saves byte-identical); 19 tests
- [x] (vii-b) Engine read path: volume/pan lanes ŌĆö `AutomationSchedule`/`AutomationRenderer` (atomic slot + Ōēź1s retire bin, MIDIEventSchedule pattern; preallocated cursors w/ binary-search reseek), post-chain-walk gain+pan stage in ChainHostAU + InstrumentRenderer (per-sample linear ramps ŌĆö analytic bounce error 7.4e-9; pan-center bit-exact null), fader-override (mixer pinned, lane supplies gain; mute/solo gating intact) + stopped-WYSIWYG, no-restart point republish (proven: MIDI schedule object identity unchanged across mid-play edits), live/offline parity cross-diff 0.0; 9 engine tests
- [x] (vii-c) Engine read path: built-in FX-param lanes ŌĆö per-quantum render-thread POD stores (quantum-start eval, `AutomationParamOverlay` base/effective split w/ knob-revert on lane removal, 64-track/strip cap matching preallocated cursors); lock-free-POD audit per kind (all nine: main-actor apply allocates ŌåÆ lean render-thread setter added; derive paths pure libm/arithmetic, limiter lookahead fixed-size, delay/reverb/chorus lines MAX-sized read-offset changes)
- [x] (vii-d) Control protocol + MCP ŌĆö `automation.addLane|removeLane|setPoints|setLaneEnabled` (target/point wire shapes round-trip through the model's own Codable so wire never drifts from persistence; per-index point parse errors; store rejections surface verbatim), snapshot lanes ride Track's encoding for free, 12 control tests, 4 MCP tools (51 total) with AI-agent-oriented descriptions
- [x] (vii-e) Arrange automation lane UI (v0) ŌĆö per-track disclosure row (cyan-glow glyph when lanes active), VOL/PAN target picker + green enable toggle + delete, Canvas breakpoint editor (neon polyline w/ glow, click-add, drag-move w/ live readout, double-click/Ōī½ delete, dimmed when disabled; pan lanes neutral-white per mixer convention); pure geometry/edit/selection logic headless in `DAWAppKit.AutomationLaneModel` (16 tests); all edits via vii-a store methods (per-tick drag commits ride the `automation.points:<laneID>` coalescing key); debug-tier `ui.showAutomation` for headless capture; pattern codified in DESIGN-LANGUAGE.md ŌĆö **automation v0 complete** (vii-f deferred)
- [ ] (vii-f) DEFERRED post-v0: touch/latch/write recording, sendLevel engine support, AU-param lanes, master lanes, bezier curves
- [x] (viii-a) PDC plan math (DAWCore) ŌĆö `LatencyCompensation.swift`: `PDCPlan.compute(input:cap:)` (`PDCStripKind.track(outputsToMaster:hasSends:)|.bus`, per-strip plannedSamples/compensationSamples/clamped/skewSamples + residual, T/B/maxPathLatency; bypass-stable maxima over all-effects sums, comp from active sums, sends pin to T, no-sends direct-to-master refinement to T+B, skew=B only for direct+sends while B>0, 16384 cap w/ honest unclamped reporting, hostile negative inputs clamped not precondition-crashed); 15 unit tests incl. spec worked example verbatim
- [x] (viii-b) Compensation ring (DAWEngine) ŌĆö `CompensationDelay.swift` (`CompensationDelayState`: 32768-float pow-2 rings/channel, heap atomic target+resetFlag, render-only writeIndex/appliedOffset/historyClean; clean-history target-0 fast path provably buffer-untouched; dirty target-0 keeps writing so later retargets crossfade into real history); inserted in ChainHostAU between chain walk and automation.apply + InstrumentRenderer main AND idle paths; `PlaybackGraph.setCompensationTarget(_:forStrip:)` + `armCompensationResets()` at stopAllPlayers/startAllPlayers (covers cold start + offline start; v0 loop wrap flushes BY DESIGN ŌĆö wrap is a restart where chain tails already cut; spec's no-flush rule applies when seamless wrap lands); 7 tests: impulse alignment 4800/5040ŌåÆsingle coherent 0.5 peak, exact null, 512-bit-pattern inertness, bit-exact crossfade formula, reset kills 240-sample stale tail, determinism, instrument-path 480
- [x] (viii-c) PDC recompute wiring + reporting ŌĆö single choke point at the tail of `PlaybackGraph.applyParameters` (all 6 trigger events already funnel through it; offline calls it both sides of engine start ŌåÆ parity by construction); `EffectChainState.latencySamplesAllEffects`; `PDCReport` (outputLatency structured for a future master chain); additive snapshot fields (per-strip chainLatencySamples/compensationSamples always, clamped/skew omit-if-false/zero; project `pdc` object); no new command (spec ┬¦6, snapshots ride existing surface; MCP passthrough untyped so no TS change); 7 wiring tests + live E2E 23/23 (bypass mid-play: totals stable, one-strip retarget, playback never stops)
- [x] (viii-d) PDC parity ŌĆö latent-chain + shared-send-bus project cross-diffed across two offline renders at bit-level 0.0 with plan-correct 4-path coherent alignment (peak exactly 1.0); live-capture harness doesn't exist yet, so v0 bar = offline determinism + live E2E assertions (honest note); ARCHITECTURE settled entry landed at design time; strip latency-readout DESIGN note deferred to when the mixer grows the readout ŌĆö **M4 (viii) PDC v0 COMPLETE**

## M5 ŌĆö Editing depth
- [x] (i-a) Clip edit domain + store ŌĆö `Clip.gainDb` (ŌłÆ72ŌĆ”+24) + `fadeInBeats`/`fadeOutBeats` + `FadeCurve.linear|equalPower` + NEW `startOffsetSeconds` (didn't exist; split/trim impossible without it), all additive omit-when-default Codable incl. ClipDocument mirror (pre-edit projects byte-identical); pure `envelopeGain(atBeat:)` (equal-power sin/cos quarter-cycle, gain├Śfades multiplicative ŌĆö midpoints 0.5 / 0.7071 / ŌłÆ6dBŌēł0.5012 verified); store ops splitClip (fixed-tempo offset math + MIDI partition w/ overhang truncation + fade redistribution), trimClip (leading edge advances offset, drops outside notes, re-clamps fades), moveClip, setClipGain, setClipFades ŌĆö clamped, undo-coalesced (`clip.trim|move|gain|fades:<id>`), proportional fade reduction when in+out > length; 17 tests / 3 suites
- [x] (i-b) Clip gain/fade engine read path ŌĆö settled design implemented: `ClipFadeBake.swift` (piecePlan contiguity by construction, applyEnvelope from `Clip.envelopeGain` w/ gain zeroed, bake-owned second AVAudioFile reader ŌĆö never the player's stateful streaming instance); scheduleAll three-piece buffer/segment/buffer (unfaded = pre-i-b byte-identical path; bake failure ŌåÆ unfaded fallback, timing over shape), startOffsetSeconds honored (bit-exact), gain = player.volume every applyParameters pass + in-place `clipGainChanged` (no restart; gainDb in NO reconcile signature; fades/offset ARE schedule-affecting ŌåÆ restart+re-bake); MIDI clips unreachable by construction; 12 tests: fade error 0.0, null 0/96000 frames, splice-invariance residue 2.98e-8 (1 ulp), equal-power Ōēż +3.02 dB, mid-fade start exact, determinism
- [x] (i-c) Clip edit control + MCP ŌĆö `clip.split|trim|move|setGain|setFades` (split returns both clips; parseFadeCurve names the offending field; store rejections verbatim), 5 MCP tools (56 total), 14 control tests, live E2E 24/24 (split note partition, snapshot round-trips, persistence, error surfaces) re-run independently ALL PASS
- [x] (i-d) Waveform editor UI ŌĆö interactive ClipBlock (body drag = snapped move, ~6pt edge zones = snapped trim, double-click/context-menu split incl. at-playhead, corner fade grips w/ translucent linear/equal-power shading + alt-click curve toggle via context menu, cyan dB gain chip w/ vertical drag), SNAP header control (Off/Bar/Beat/1/2/1/4 ŌĆö Bar follows the meter, hence new ClipSnap not the piano roll's fixed-bar SnapResolution), `ClipWaveform` cached off-main peak outline windowed by startOffsetSeconds; headless `ClipEditModel` in DAWAppKit (snap/hit/preview math mirroring store clamps, 14 tests); all edits via the five store methods; capture-verified (split visible, fades bowed, waveform continuous across split, ŌłÆ6.0 dB chips) ŌĆö **M5 (i) waveform editor COMPLETE** (44 tests total across i-aŌĆ”d)

- [x] (ii-b) Vendor + facade ŌĆö signalsmith-stretch v1.3.2 (57b93f4) + signalsmith-linear (7f53cdd) vendored verbatim w/ licenses + VENDORED.md pins; `CSignalsmithStretch` target (flat-C nullability-annotated API, one C++ TU, Accelerate backend, package cxx17 ŌĆö no conflicts); `OfflineStretcher` facade (planar core + PCM-buffer convenience, upstream `exact()` recipe via output_seek ŌåÆ no post-trim, FIXED RNG seed ŌåÆ determinism + content-keyed-cache-ready, `isIdentity` bypass predicate excludes formant per seam rule); 8 tests: lengths EXACT (144000/72000/96000), pitch 440ŌåÆ440.00 / +7stŌåÆ659.00 vs 659.26, formant variant, cancellation at poll 2 of ~36, bit-identical runs; FLAG for ii-d/e: 0.75├Ś overlap-add overshoot peak 1.414 from 0.8 input (~+4.9 dB) ŌĆö Float32 CAF won't clip on disk but headroom decision needed at listening spike

  - [x] (crash-a) Teardown crash: root-cause + fix + regression guard ŌĆö **FIXED 2026-07-10 (root cause PROVEN with a 6-experiment live evidence matrix, not conjectured)**: mechanism = AVFoundation completes a node detach's internal graph bookkeeping ONLY when it can synchronize with a running engine; detaching a once-rendered node while STOPPED leaves a stale raw `AUGraphNodeBaseV3*` in `AVAudioEngineGraph`'s internal list (survives `reset()`+`start()`; explicit disconnect-first does NOT purge it ŌĆö experiments D1/D2), ARC then frees the node, and the next live `connect` (first track.add after project.new) walks freed memory. Our teardown hit it because reconcile's removal pass fires the quiesce-STOP at the first non-trivial strip, so the mass detach ran stopped-after-running. KEY INVERSION (exp C): stop-before-any-detach ŌĆö the "cleanest" reading of the old discipline ŌĆö still crashes; the discipline's stop IS the poison for detaches (safe direction is attach-while-stopped/cold-start; detach needs RUNNING ŌĆö exp B/E clean incl. a full 28-strip live teardown). H2 refuted (every removed node had a paired detach); H3 not the trigger but the fix restores the detach-sync guarantee the renderer-deinit WATCH item leans on. FIX (minimal): `PlaybackGraph.retireNode(_:)`/`flushRetiredNodes()` + `engineHasRun` ŌĆö running or never-ran ŌåÆ detach now (offline/test byte-identical); stopped-after-running ŌåÆ park attached+strongly-held in a FIFO pending-detach bin (no freed-memory window CAN exist), flushed after every successful `engine.start()` (prepare/rewire-bounce/config-recovery) + defensively at reconcile entry; every teardown detach site seam-routed incl. dead `detachAll()`; announce/bounce semantics untouched; silently covers latent same-class windows (live addSend old-gain teardown, invalidateInstrumentNode, mixed bus-removal passes). Root-cause note + evidence matrix: `docs/research/fix-teardown-crash.md` (written BEFORE the fix); repro doc status FIXED; ARCHITECTURE boundary discipline gained the lifetime rule. ## M11 ŌĆö Pro-parity round 1 (seeded 2026-07-11 from the m10-q audit, docs/research/audit-m10q-pro-parity.md)

Ranked by the audit's payoff/effort ├Ś AI-native alignment. Every capability item ships the house vertical: store method + control command + MCP tool + tests + (where visual) captures.

- [x] (m11-d) Arrange-level clip crossfades + overlap correctness ŌĆö **COMPLETE 2026-07-11**. Fixes the audit's NEW-DISCOVERY BUG (`ProjectStore.moveClip` did no overlap detection ŌåÆ overlapped ordinary clips silently volume-doubled with no crossfade/error) AND ships a crossfade tool. **Policy (settled, no render change): ┬¦1** no SILENT overlap of ordinary same-track clips ŌĆö only the explicit crossfade tool creates a legitimate overlap (covered by complementary fades); **┬¦2** a move that lands on a stationary same-track clip TRIMS the covered region (full containment ŌåÆ the stationary clip is removed), audio+MIDI alike, comp members exempt, all inside ONE "Move Clip" undo; **┬¦3** m10-k targeted-track import applies the same trim inside its single-undo batch (new-track placements unaffected); **┬¦4** moving a previously-crossfaded clip re-trims against current boundaries, fades survive as plain per-clip fades. **DAWCore**: value types `ClipMoveResult {clip, trimmedClipIDs, removedClipIDs}` + `CrossfadeResult {left, right, overlapBeats}`; `moveClip` rewritten to rebuild the lane applying `resolveOverlap` to each ordinary (non-comp-member) same-track clip; statics `clipTrimmedToWindow` (mirrors `trimClip`: advances `startOffsetSeconds`, drops/truncates MIDI, clamps fades; nil below `minClipLengthBeats`) + `resolveOverlap` (disjointŌåÆkeep / full-coverŌåÆdrop / head-coverŌåÆtrim leading / tail-or-insideŌåÆtrim trailing); `crossfadeClips(trackId, clipId, otherClipId, lengthBeats)` ŌĆö AUDIO only, adjacent or overlapping Ōēż length, symmetric half-each extension where source material exists (else field-named `crossfadeNeedsMaterial`), legacy-overlap normalization, complementary `equalPower` fades spanning EXACTLY the final overlap, each clip's OTHER fade preserved, ONE "Crossfade Clips" undo; `importAudioBatch` existing-track path now applies `resolveOverlap`. **Wire (+1, 114ŌåÆ115)**: `clip.crossfade {trackId, clipId, otherClipId, lengthBeats>0}` ŌåÆ `{left, right, overlapBeats}` (field-named errors `crossfadeNotEligible`/`crossfadeNeedsMaterial`); `clip.move` response gained additive `trimmed:[UUID]`/`removed:[UUID]` (existing `clip` fields byte-identical). **MCP (+1, 117ŌåÆ118)**: `clip_crossfade` teaching the splitŌåÆbuttŌåÆcrossfade workflow; `clip_move` description carries the overlap policy + the additive fields. **Copilot catalog 43ŌåÆ44** (clip 11ŌåÆ12; `clip.crossfade` added, non-destructive-beyond-undo). **UI**: arrange clip context menu **"Crossfade with Next"** (┬╝/┬Į/1/2-beat submenu, audio-only, only when a crossfadeable next clip exists) ŌåÆ `ProjectStore.crossfadeClips`; a green **X-bowtie seam badge** over each overlapping ordinary audio pair (the clips' own fade wedges shade the overlap ŌĆö neutral audio green, never violet); `.crossfade` Explain entry (catalog **61ŌåÆ62**). **Explain overlay robustness (thin-view fix, general)**: `ExplainOverlay.cardCenter` now clamps the card center in BOTH axes so a card flipping above a high anchor (e.g. the seam badge near the ruler) can no longer clip its title off the window top. `debug.explainMode {focus:"crossfade"}` stages the capture. **GATE (staging 17695, headless WS driver)**: suite **1908/222** (+ `DAWCoreTests.ClipCrossfadeTests` 13, `DAWControlTests.ClipCrossfadeCommandTests` 7), 0 warnings incl. `--build-tests`; npm **84/84** (0 skipped, 118-tool pin exercised); live gate ALL PASS ŌĆö **(a) doubling fixed, MEASURED**: single clip **ŌłÆ10.66 LUFS**, a second identical clip stacked on top **ŌłÆ4.64 LUFS** (the pre-fix bug reproduced, **+6.02 dB**), then a 50 %-overlap move trimmed the stationary clip ŌåÆ **ŌłÆ10.63 LUFS** (**afterVsSingle 0.03 dB ŌĆö doubling gone**), `clip.move` returned `trimmed:[clipA]`; **(b) crossfade proof**: `overlapBeats 1`, both fades `equalPower` == overlap, windowed continuity across two DECORRELATED noise clips **ŌłÆ10.66 / ŌłÆ10.67 / ŌłÆ10.69 LUFS** (**seam spread 0.03 dB** ŌĆö seamless), `edit.history` top **"Crossfade Clips"** (ONE step) and undo reverted the fade, needs-material error field-named ("clip 'noiseA' has no audio before its startŌĆ”"); **(c) import overlap**: `debug.importAudio` onto a resident clip ŌåÆ 2 clips, resident trimmed 8ŌåÆ**4 beats**, **no overlap**, one batch undo "Import 'noiseA'". Pixel-reviewed captures: the crossfaded seam with the X-bowtie + crossing fade wedges, and the `.crossfade` Explain card. **DEVIATIONS**: (1) the "Crossfade with Next" **context menu is not captured** ŌĆö `debug.captureUI` uses `cacheDisplay`, which cannot render an AppKit `NSMenu` popup (the menu item + Explain copy stand in as evidence); (2) equal-power crossfades hold constant POWER only for DECORRELATED material ŌĆö identical/correlated material sums coherently (+3 dB), so gate (b) uses two independent noise files, not a split of one file (documented in the gate + command doc). Wire surface now **115 cmds / 118 tools**, Copilot catalog **44**, Explain **62**. **UPDATE (orchestrator verification):** independent suite re-runs green ŌĆö Swift 1908/222, npm 84/84 explicit (0 skipped); counts re-verified (allCommands 115, registerTool 118, ExplainID 62, catalog carries clip.crossfade); all three captures pixel-reviewed (seam bowtie + crossing wedges, fully-rendered Explain card); OWN independently-authored render-and-measure gate on a DIFFERENT scenario (0.5-beat crossfade vs the agent's 1-beat; trim-then-move-adjacent construction) passed ALL checks ŌĆö post-trim span LUFS **identical** to the single-clip reference (ŌłÆ10.6288 both), `clip.move` reported `trimmed:[ŌĆ”]`, overlap exactly 0.5 with equalPower fades == overlap, seam spread **0.03 dB** across decorrelated noise, one-step "Crossfade Clips" undo reverting the fades, needs-material error verbatim (scratchpad verify-m11d-xfade.mjs). Render-and-land vertical over `ProjectStore.bounceTrackInPlace(trackId, fromBeat?, durationSeconds?, muteSource?, name?)` (`Sources/DAWCore/ProjectStore+Bounce.swift`), reusing `render.stems`' render machinery (full-session forced PDC, single post-fader `StemPlan.passTracks` pass, same default window, NEVER normalized ŌĆö DAWEngine untouched) and `importGeneration`'s land discipline (render+write OUTSIDE the edit body into the project-stable `generationImportsDirectory`; ONE `performEdit("Bounce in Place")` inserts the `<source> (Bounced)` audio track+clip DIRECTLY AFTER the source and mutes the source when `muteSource` default-true). Eligibility is IDENTICAL to `render.stems` for one track (`StemPlan.descriptors`): bus-routed source ŌåÆ `stemNotMasterInput` verbatim, unknown ŌåÆ `trackNotFound`, empty window ŌåÆ `nothingToRender`; a bus bounces. Undo removes the new track+clip AND restores the source's prior mute; the rendered FILE stays on disk (import semantics). `renderCompletedCount` deliberately NOT ticked (that's the export-song onboarding signal). Result `BounceInPlaceResult {track, clip, file, sourceTrackId, sourceMuted, measurement}`. **Wire (+1, 115ŌåÆ116)**: `track.bounceInPlace`. **MCP (+1, 118ŌåÆ119)**: `track_bounce_in_place`; NOT in the Copilot catalog (long-running render op ŌĆö the `render.*` exclusion precedent, documented). **UI**: track-header context menu "Bounce in Place" (master-input tracks only, both densities ŌĆö no density split, no inventory row); Explain `.bounceInPlace` (catalog 62ŌåÆ**63**). - [x] (m13-h2) **Envelope-bake perf follow-up** (filed from the m13-e audio-dsp review ŌĆö correctness is NOT at stake, the null/analytic gates all pass): a non-empty gain envelope currently converts the clip's bake plan to ONE full-region baked piece, so `bakePiece` (PlaybackGraph.swift ~:1710) allocates and per-frame-evaluates the entire scheduled region on the main actor at EVERY `scheduleAll` (play/seek/loop restart) ŌĆö ~230 MB + ~29 M `envelopeGain` calls (per-frame `pow` + O(points) scan) for a 10-min stereo 48 k clip. Candidate fixes (pick via measurement, audio-dsp-engineer): piecewise bake only the inter-point spans whose gain ŌēĀ unity (mirror the fade three-piece plan), hoist the dBŌåÆlinear `pow` to per-ramp incremental multiplication, and/or cache the baked buffer keyed by (file, shape, envelope) across scheduleAll calls. Also inherits the reviewer's note that the pre-existing bake-failure catch fallback (PlaybackGraph.swift ~:1727-1734) now silently drops the envelope too ("timing wins", stderr-logged) ŌĆö decide if that deserves a user-visible warning. GATE: perf measurement before/after on a long enveloped clip (bake time + peak RSS at scheduleAll), null-case byte gate era, analytic envelope render tests unchanged. ŌĆö **COMPLETE 2026-07-12 (audio-dsp-engineer).** Fix chosen BY MEASUREMENT: **piecewise bake** (`ClipFadeBake.envelopedPiecePlan` + `PlaybackGraph.scheduleEnvelopedPieces`) ŌĆö only spans the envelope/fades actually shape are baked (┬▒1 guard frame, streamed gaps < 8_192 frames fold into the bake); provably-unity spans stream straight off the file, bit-identical to the old `├Ś 1.0` multiply, so rendered bytes are UNCHANGED in every case (not just null). MEASURED (release, 10-min stereo 48 k clip, 4-beat dip, `OfflineRenderer` 0.25 s pull ŌēĪ one scheduleAll): mostly-unity **191.5 ms ŌåÆ 40.6 ms** median (dry floor 38.8 ms; bake cost ~153 ms ŌåÆ ~1.5 ms), peak RSS **287 MB ŌåÆ 20 MB** (dry 18 MB); flat-0 dB envelope 203 ŌåÆ 39.2 ms (zero bake); full-non-unity stays ~205 ms/284 MB (envelope genuinely shapes everything ŌĆö honest cost; pow-hoist + cache REJECTED: read+alloc dominates, numerics/invalidation risk buys nothing in the common case). Byte gates all four SHA-identical before/after (null `0adcccbdŌĆ”`, enveloped `83f2e4c1ŌĆ”`, mid-seek `3d939bf3ŌĆ”`, Bus Song bundle COPY `1d9e5e3fŌĆ”`); m13-e analytic/null tests pass UNMODIFIED (unity-envelope residue now exactly 0.0). Fallback decision: bake failure stays stderr-only (clip still sounds on time; failure = transient second-reader I/O on a file the player already opened) but the message now says explicitly it drops envelope AND fades; follow-up to file = engine-notices surface for schedule-time degradations. ## M14 ŌĆö Gapless loop wrap (seeded 2026-07-12 from the m13-f design spike: docs/research/design-m13f-gapless-loop.md, GO-WITH-CONDITIONS; implementation follows that doc's ┬¦9 phases L-1ŌĆ”L-4 and ┬¦10 conditions C1ŌĆōC8 verbatim ŌĆö deviations return to the design doc for amendment)

Offline/render parity (┬¦7): nothing changes offline, ever ŌĆö provably (C8).

## M15 ŌĆö Post-gapless correctness & agent-ergonomics round (seeded 2026-07-13 from the post-M14 audit: docs/research/audit-m15.md, 12 findings F1ŌĆōF12, 2 measured live bugs; orchestrator spot-checked the F1 both-call-sites citation, the F8 dismissal evidence, and the F5 mechanism before authoring) ŌĆö **MILESTONE COMPLETE 2026-07-13 (aŌĆōg all verified)**

- [x] (m15-a) **Metronome meter-map correctness ŌĆö the audit's HIGH measured bug (F1).** The live click ignores meter changes: with 4/4ŌåÆ3/4 at beat 8, downbeats land at 0,4,8,12,16,20 (constant 4/4) instead of 0,4,8,11,14,17,20 ŌĆö measured via debug.masterCapture amplitude+frequency classification of all 23 clicks. Mechanism: `AudioEngine.clickMeterMap` builds `MeterMap(constant:)` from the cached `beatsPerBar` scalar (AudioEngine.swift:1607-1609; cache :1478) ŌĆö and `OfflineRenderer.swift:246` does the SAME (its in-code claim "offline callers pass real maps" is FALSE ŌĆö only tests pass real maps); count-in inherits the scalar too (wrong bar length in a non-base meter, code-proven). Fix: plumb the REAL `store.transport.meterMap` through both call sites + count-in; the Metronome API is already fully MeterMap-aware (m14-c) so this is plumbing, S-sized, control-plane only. Route: audio-dsp-engineer. GATE: the audit's capture probe re-run verbatim ŌĆö live 4/4ŌåÆ3/4 downbeats at 0,4,8,11,14,17,20 by amplitude+frequency classification; offline render click positions == the meter map; count-in bar length correct in 3/4; C8-style null era (constant-meter project byte-identical); the m14-c meter pin extended to the LIVE path. ŌĆö **COMPLETE 2026-07-13, ALL GATES PASS** (audio-dsp-engineer). Production surface = 4 files. AudioEngine.swift: the cached `beatsPerBar` scalar is GONE from the engine (it existed solely for the click map + count-in) ŌĆö `cacheTransportFlags` caches the WHOLE `transport.meterMap` as the stored `clickMeterMap` (a trivial project synthesizes the constant map, so the null case is arithmetic-identical), the computed constant-map property and its false comment DELETED, all four live schedule sites read the cache, count-in derives bar length from it. - [ ] (m17-i) **MLX-native ACE-Step spike (research first; user asked 2026-07-16 whether the model can be embedded natively via Apple Neural Engine/MLX instead of the external sidecar).** Position recorded: ANE (Core ML) is NOT viable for this model class (multi-billion-param diffusion transformer; ANE wants small static-shape fp16 nets) ŌĆö the plausible native path is MLX on the GPU. IN-PROCESS embedding stays REJECTED regardless of framework: the main process owns the RT audio engine, a model spiking tens of GB of unified memory + GPU contention in-process risks dropouts, and a model crash must never be a DAW crash (M16 lesson) ŌĆö heavy AI belongs out-of-process. The REAL candidate: replace the Python/FastAPI sidecar with a NATIVE MLX helper process (mlx-swift, or minimal Python-MLX as a stepping stone) IF a quality MLX port of ACE-Step-1.5 exists. Research **DELIVERED 2026-07-16** (docs/research/2026-07-16-ace-mlx-native.md; orchestrator spot-checked the ACEStepClient:16-26 citation ŌĆö exact, the sidecar speaks ACE-Step's upstream job-queue API): **VERDICT NO-GO on a Swift/mlx-swift helper now ŌĆö WAIT.** No diffusion-music model class exists in Swift MLX anywhere (mlx-swift-examples = LLM/VLM/embeddings/SD-image only; mlx-audio-swift = TTS/STT/STS/codecs); every existing ACE-Step MLX path (official 1.5 hybrid, `mlx-community/ACE-Step1.5-MLX` weights via mlx-audio, community forks) terminates in Python; cold-start is weight-load-dominated (8ŌĆō20+ GB from disk ŌĆö a Swift rewrite pays the same), and the ANE ceiling is confirmed ~1ŌĆō1.3B params (Core ML SD precedent) vs ACE-Step's 5ŌĆō9B+ pipeline. RE-CHECK trigger: mlx-audio-swift or mlx-swift-examples shipping ANY diffusion-audio model class. - [ ] (m18-i) **Open piano-roll editor renders stale content after wire/arrange-side clip geometry ops (filed: m18-e orchestrator disjoint gate, 2026-07-16).** With the piano roll OPEN on a clip, a wire-driven `clip.trim` (extend OR shorten) leaves the ENTIRE editor stale ŌĆö notes, VEL lane, controller strip, and the CTRL readout all keep drawing the pre-trim clip (including points/notes the store has already dropped; readout shows a deleted point's value) until the clip is re-selected; a decoy-reselect renders the new state perfectly. Evidence: m18e-orch/ captures ŌĆö g2-relit.png/g3-trimmed.png (stale, open editor: 13-beat clip still drawn with a beat-8 boundary; 4-beat clip still drawing 7 points while the analytic snapshot read shows 3) vs r2-relit-reopened.png/r4-trimmed-reopened.png (correct after reselect). Editor-internal edits and `clip.setControllerLane` refresh fine ŌĆö the gap is specifically the arrange-side/wire geometry mutation path not being in the open editor's invalidation set. This matters MORE here than in a human-only DAW: AI agents mutate clips over the wire while a human watches the editor ŌĆö the view must never show dead data. Scope: find the piano-roll editor's clip-observation seam, add trim/move/split-class mutations to it (or observe the store's clip identity+geometry properly); NO new wire surface. Route: swift-app-engineer. GATE: re-run `m18e-orch/orch-relight.mjs` UNCHANGED ŌĆö the g2 capture must show all points re-lit with the boundary at beat 13 and g3 must show exactly three lit points and nothing beyond beat 4, WITHOUT any reselect; plus a regression test for the observation seam if it's model-side testable; suites Ōēź2568/292, pins held.

## M19 ŌĆö Sampler deep import (seeded 2026-07-16 from the m18-h design spike: docs/research/2026-07-16-spike-sfz-dspreset-design.md, GO, 10ŌĆō11 days across four independently shippable items; implementation follows that doc's frozen ┬¦2.2 tier table + ┬¦2.3 degradation policy verbatim ŌĆö deviations return to the design doc for amendment. Runs after M18 completes (m18-i remains). Additional M19 items will be seeded from the standing rider pool at M18 close.)

- [ ] (m19-a) **Sampler selection dimension: velocity layers, groups, round-robin, random.** Additive-optional `SamplerZone` fields (`minVelocity`/`maxVelocity`/`group`/`seqLength`/`seqPosition`/`randMin`/`randMax`, nil = today's behavior exactly) + `parseSampler`/MCP `samplerZoneSchema` ride-along + engine selection per design ┬¦4.2 (group-sorted zones, one voice per group per note-on, RR counters + seeded xorshift as render-thread-owned runtime state per ┬¦4.3) + voice pool 16ŌåÆ64. Route: audio-dsp-engineer. GATE: new SamplerSelectionTests (velocity routing, deterministic RR rotation over 8 triggers, seeded random partition, two-group layering RMS, 64-voice oldest-steal) + the existing SamplerTests suite UNCHANGED and green (legacy zones = implicit group 0 must select byte-identically).
- [ ] (m19-b) **Per-zone playback scalars + 4-stage envelope.** `tuneCents`/`pan`/`ampVelTrack`/`oneShot`/`startFrame`/`endFrame`/`attack`/`decay`/`sustain`/`release` per design ┬¦4.4ŌĆō4.5 (PolySynth `Stage`-machine pattern copy, per-voice coefficients computed at trigger, constant-power pan on the existing two-channel path, nil fields collapse to today's exact attackŌåÆholdŌåÆrelease). Route: audio-dsp-engineer. GATE: staged envelope/pan render measurements + legacy suite unchanged-green.
- [ ] (m19-c) **SFZ importer + import surface.** `Sources/DAWCore/SampleLibraries/`: SFZPreprocessor (`#include` depth-capped/cycle-detected + `#define` with structured aborts, ┬¦5.1/┬¦5.4) + SFZParser (tokenizer warts as first-class tests: spaces in sample paths, note names, comments, CRLF, dB values, header inheritance) + SampleLibraryMapper (the ENTIRE ┬¦2.3 degradation policy in one place, emits `SampleLibraryImportReport` w/ byte accounting: warn Ōēź500 MB, refuse >4 GB sans force) + `instrument.importSampleLibrary` wire command (journaled project mutation ŌĆö deliberately unlike library-only `instrument.importSoundBank`) + `instrument_import_sample_library` MCP twin + panel hook + docs (public support matrix per sfizz norm; FREE-INSTRUMENTS row; ARCHITECTURE SETTLED entry; copy law: "imports .sfz (documented subset) and .dspreset files", never "DecentSampler-compatible"). Route: swift-app-engineer (parser/mapper/store/panel) + mcp-integration-engineer (wire/MCP surface). GATE: mini-Salamander-topology fixture (wrapper + includes + defines) imports; E2E offline render RMS gate (importSampleLibrary ŌåÆ clip.addMIDI ŌåÆ render.measureLoudness); pins 126ŌåÆ127 wire / 129ŌåÆ130 MCP.
- [ ] (m19-d) **`.dspreset` importer.** DSPresetParser (Foundation XMLDocument) onto the shared IR ŌĆö mapper/report/command dispatch all reused from m19-c; `<ui>`/`<midi>`/`<effects>` ignored by design ("plays as authored"). Route: swift-app-engineer. GATE: fixture parity tests + E2E render gate. (v2 candidates stay FILED, not boxed: loops + WAV `smpl`-chunk fallback; `.dslibrary` unzip; streaming/background sample load; reference-in-place library persistence policy.)

## Blocked

- **M10 (m10-p-1ŌĆ”6) voice conversion ŌĆö HuggingFace large-binary fetch blocked by corp TLS-interception proxy** ŌĆö noted 2026-07-11 at the m10-p-1 spike: every neural asset RVC needs (ContentVec/HuBERT encoder 360.8 MB, RMVPE pitch extractor 172.8 MB, generic non-personal Applio base pretrains 69.7/136.3 MB) lives on HF's LFS/CDN path, which hard-times-out under the proxy on every route tried (direct `huggingface.co/resolve/ŌĆ”`, `hf-mirror.com`, HTTP/1.1 forced). Plain PyPI and HF's small API/raw endpoints work fine ŌĆö this is specifically a large-binary/LFS block, and it gates inference AND training identically on either engine (same files). Everything software-side is already proven (venv recipe, MLX GPU + MPS backends live ŌĆö see docs/research/spike-m10p-vc.md incl. exact URLs/byte sizes in "Exact install shape for p-2"). PRECEDENT: the 55 GB ACE-Step weights DID download onto this machine previously ŌĆö the block is likely a network-window condition (e.g. corp VPN on/off), not permanent. To unblock: on an unproxied network, fetch the four files from `huggingface.co/IAHispano/Applio` per the spike doc and re-run the spike's measurement half (fast ŌĆö install is reproducible), then p-2ŌĆ”p-6 proceed. Also resolve before shipping: the MLX fork's missing LICENSE file (pyproject claims MIT; `gh repo view` licenseInfo null).
- ~~M4 (i) live mid-play send activation~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-06** (diagnostic round 3, per the parked method: stderr instrumentation + node-connection dump + preallocated-atomic tap probes + the live `diag-send.mjs` repro). Root cause was NOT the send wiring: the connection dump immediately after the rewire resume showed the mid-play-added leg fully attached and connected (source mixer ŌåÆ gain(vol 0.5) ŌåÆ bus sum ŌåÆ chain host ŌåÆ bus mixer, 48 kHz/2ch throughout) and the gain node's tap FIRING ŌĆö carrying peak 0.0. Two stacked mechanisms produced the "silent until stop/play" symptom, on ALL strips (bus A metered 0.0000 after the resume too ŌĆö the old E2E's poll windows just never caught it): (1) **THE BUG** ŌĆö the resume anchored `derivedBeats` on `outputNode.lastRenderTime`, which right after the stopŌåÆresetŌåÆstart bounce still reports the PREVIOUS render session's sample clock (valid flags set, measured sample=98304) while the restarted session's clock begins again near 0; the `max()` clamp then froze the playhead at the resume beat for the ENTIRE prior session length (unbounded in a long session ŌĆö why it read as "silent forever"), postponing the loop-wrap revival past every poll (predicted wrap +4.19 s vs observed +4.17 s, 36 ms match). (2) The repro material (7.5-beat sustained MIDI chord) has no note-on between the resume beat and the wrap, and no-chase is the settled v0 contract (`MIDIEventSchedule`, ARCHITECTURE.md), so the resumed schedule was legitimately silent until the wrap ŌĆö "stop/play revives it" was simply a restart from beat 0 with fresh note-ons, not a topology repair. FIX (one flag): the rewire resume calls `startPlayers(ŌĆ”, renderClockTrusted: false)`, forcing the already-proven host-clock anchor branch (host time is monotonic across the bounce; players start on hostTime anchors in both branches, so nothing else changes). Live post-fix: MIDI pad send meters on B at +2.29 s (= the wrap, level exactly matching the stop/play reference, no transport command, A uninterrupted-then-revived per the restart contract); audio-clip send meters at +0.26 s with A continuously intact; bus E2E 19/19 (fx-poll window widened to cover the no-chase wrap, with comment); suite 920/117 green; app stderr clean.
- ~~Teardown crash: `project.new` after a played send/bus project~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-12 (m13-a) ŌĆö the crash class is dead BY CONSTRUCTION: once-rendered engines are never surgically detached; teardown-class changes discard and rebuild the whole engine.** Full arc, kept as the institutional record: **(1) 2026-07-06, discovery** during M4 (i) verification ŌĆö build trackŌåÆbusA output + sendŌåÆbusB, `transport.play` ~1 s, `stop`, `project.new`, next `track.add` ŌåÆ SIGSEGV inside `-[AVAudioEngine connect:to:format:]` ŌåÆ `AVAudioEngineGraph::UpdateGraphAfterReconfig` ŌåÆ `swift_unknownObjectRelease` on a garbage pointer (`DAWApp-2026-07-06-051956.ips`; a sibling run crashed in a SwiftUI executor check, `ŌĆ”-051559.ips` ŌĆö two surface stacks = heap corruption); the never-played variant did not crash. **(2) 2026-07-10, M9 crash-a fix** ŌĆö diagnosis "detach against a stopped engine is unsafe"; mechanism = retire bin (`pendingDetachNodes` parked while stopped, `flushRetiredNodes()` after restart); live-verified 3├Ś that day. **(3) 2026-07-12, FALSIFICATION** ŌĆö the M13 audit (audit-m13.md B1) hit 3/3 staging sessions SIGSEGV'ing inside the fix's OWN flush path, and the m13-a C0 instrumented experiment named the mechanism with node-level evidence: after ONE engine stopŌåÆresetŌåÆstart boundary, the FIRST flush-detach ŌĆö of the routed source's strip mixer, with the engine RUNNING and `isRunning=true` logged at the call ŌĆö is itself the faulting frame (instrumented addr `0x9ba885060 AVAudioMixerNode`, no survive line, `DAWApp-2026-07-12-104059.ips`; independently reproduced via `track.remove`, `ŌĆ”-104254.ips`). So "running at detach time" was NEVER sufficient: a node that RENDERED and then sat attached across a stopŌåÆresetŌåÆstart boundary is already stale inside `AVAudioEngineGraph`'s internal node vector, and any later detach of it faults. The audit's "m12-f regression" suspicion was WRONG ŌĆö same crash on the pre-m12-f binary; M9's 3├Ś verification was heap-reuse luck. The C0 control leg (fresh-launch `project.new` ├Ś20, engine never ran) survived 20/20, formally retiring the audit's session-3 "crash on first wire command" anomaly as mis-attribution (that shape cannot reach the crashing frame; plausible source = a foreign wire client, the documented 2026-07-11 staging-port anomaly). **(4) Resolution (m13-a; design docs/research/design-m13a-teardown-crash.md, supersedes fix-teardown-crash.md)** ŌĆö retire-bin machinery deleted; announce-class reconcile on a once-rendered engine ABORTS before the first topology mutation and `AudioEngine.rebuildEngine(reason:)` discards the whole AVAudioEngine + PlaybackGraph and cold-builds from the model; `projectWillReplace()` forces the same rebuild unconditionally at project boundaries; `teardownDetach` detaches directly only against a running or never-run engine. Proven by the m13-a campaign: audit recipes verbatim + 12/12 played/unplayed ├Ś routed/plain matrix + 3├Ś 41-track perf-c + 50-cycle soak (100 rebuilds, +0.4 MB RSS) + 20├Ś fresh-launch ŌĆö zero crashes, zero new .ips, m12-b offline anchors byte-identical, worst 41-track rebuild 143 ms.
- ~~AUv3 plugin view hosting (M3 vi-b)~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-10.** Unparked once pkg-a shipped the real bundle; landed as vi-b-1 (plumbing + generic body) and vi-b-2 (vendor-view ladder) ŌĆö see the M3 checkboxes and `docs/research/design-vi-b-au-windows.md`. Residual, recorded honestly: no AUv3 exists on this machine, so the out-of-process AUv3 custom-view leg is untested by necessity (SKIPPED, never faked); the ladder degrades to the generic body + warning by design if one ever fails to serve a view.
- ~~Input device selection: pinned-device capture yields empty takes~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-05.** Root cause was NOT the eager pin wedging the AUHAL (disproved by CLI repro: eager prepare + pin still delivers tap buffers). Two stacked bugs: (1) the same-device guard compared the pin target against the AUHAL's `CurrentDevice`, which on a fresh AVAudioEngine is the engine's PRIVATE AGGREGATE device ŌĆö never equal to any raw hardware ID ŌĆö so every pinned take (default uid included) performed a real device set; (2) that set makes AVFoundation post `AVAudioEngineConfigurationChange` on the capture engine ~65 ms after start with the engine still running and the tap still healthy, and the config-change handler treated it as fatal ŌåÆ `stopRecording()` finalized the writer before the first buffer, and the writer's post-finalize guard silently swallowed every later delivery (hence zero frames AND zero stderr). Fix: pin skips when the uid resolves to the current system default (`InputDevices.defaultInputDeviceID()`); config-change handler only ends the take when the capture engine actually stopped; two-phase `InputCapture.prepare()/start(writer:)` replaces the eager pin; 1.5 s first-buffer watchdog aborts loudly ("no audio arrived from input device ŌĆ”") instead of a silent empty take. Live E2E green: default-uid pin, ZoomAudioDevice pin (frames flowed), unpinned.

To unblock: paste a key in Settings (Ōīś, ŌĆö Keychain-backed, added 2026-07-10) or set `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`/`OPENAI_API_KEY`, then run one real `ai.writeLyrics` and check the output is well-formed bracketed lyrics. Same blocker applies to the copilot rail's provider calls later in M6. **UPDATE 2026-07-11: an Anthropic key is NOW present in the Keychain** (confirmed by the beta user's real provider call, which surfaced the (m10-a) parser bug) ŌĆö this gate, rail-e, and ex-c become runnable as soon as (m10-a) lands. glass-b still waits on an OpenAI key.
